<Text>This place is truly amazing. It's run under Japanese ownership, always has since it opened. I've been going here since 1994, and although the original owner "Terry" sold it in the mid 2000's, it has not changed for the worse.

The food is always fresh and service is always friendly, polite and respectful... just like in Japan.  They greet you with the traditional "You are Honorably welcome" in Japanese.

I personally like Salmon so I order the H&D roll. It's brilliant!  Another good roll is the Crunch Roll.

The prices are fair for the amount of food they serve. The portions are big!

Make sure you order the Deep Fried Green Tea Ice Cream. You can't find it anywhere and it's to die for!!!

Cheers!

Rudy Chavarria Jr<//Text>< Pictures>

< text>
Got what you need, when you need it. Feels a bit expensive, but I think most pet store products are expensive because there are three things in life people will gladly spend enormous sums on: weddings, babies, and pets. But I digress. This store is large and well-lit. I only buy cat stuff and the selection of cat toys, food, scratchers, and beds is good. As of this writing, The Ark of San Juan cat rescue shows cats here in this store. My family has adopted two rescue cats here, both fully vaccinated, neutered, and chipped. This business relationship for PetSmart and The Ark is truly symbiotic, because one can adopt a cat (if approved) and then turn around and buy stuff from the store. This store also has a busy grooming department, and it's fun to watch the animals get groomed. They also do dog training in the store. Lots of fish and a few reptiles. Saw a chinchilla, I think, the other day. Only reason for 4 stars, rather than 5, is that often, it seems, the checkout line takes longer than it should (and I'd rate my overall patience an 9 out of 10).< /text>
